xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="18" height="18" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon text-tertiary"><path d="M4 18V14.3C4 13.4716 3.32843 12.8 2.5 12.8H2V11.2H2.5C3.32843 11.2 4 10.5284 4 9.7V6C4 4.34315 5.34315 3 7 3H8V5H7C6.44772 5 6 5.44772 6 6V10.1C6 10.9858 5.42408 11.7372 4.62623 12C5.42408 12.2628 6 13.0142 6 13.9V18C6 18.5523 6.44772 19 7 19H8V21H7C5.34315 21 4 19.6569 4 18ZM20 14.3V18C20 19.6569 18.6569 21 17 21H16V19H17C17.5523 19 18 18.5523 18 18V13.9C18 13.0142 18.5759 12.2628 19.3738 12C18.5759 11.7372 18 10.9858 18 10.1V6C18 5.44772 17.5523 5 17 5H16V3H17C18.6569 3 20 href="/docs/healthcare/transaction-enrollment">transaction enrollments</a> in your Stedi account.</p>
<p>You can filter the results by various criteria, such as a query string (fuzzy matching is supported), enrollment status, creation date, provider names, provider NPIs, provider tax IDs, and Stedi payer IDs. When a query parameter is an array, you can include it more than once in the URL to filter by multiple values.</p>
<div class="relative overflow-auto prose-no-margin my-6"><table><thead><tr><th>Query parameters</th><th>Endpoint returns</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>?providerNames=John%20Doe&amp;providerNames=Jane%20Doe</code></td><td>Enrollments associated with either John Doe or Jane Doe.</td></tr><tr><td><code>?status=LIVE</code></td><td>Enrollments in <code>LIVE</code> status.</td></tr><tr><td><code>?filter=OS&amp;createdFrom=2025-01-01T00:00:00Z</code></td><td><ul><li>Enrollments with provider names, provider NPIs, provider tax IDs, or Stedi payer IDs containing <code>os</code> or <code>OS</code>. The search is case-insensitive, and fuzzy matching is supported. </li><li>Enrollments created after <code>2025-01-01T00:00:00Z</code>.</li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></div><div class="flex text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>Filter for enrollments with properties matching a query string. You can provide all or part of a provider name, NPI, or tax ID. You can also provide all or part of a payer&#x27;s <a href="https://www.stedi.com/docs/healthcare/supported-payers#stedi-payer-id" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Stedi payer ID</a> - primary payer IDs and aliases aren&#x27;t supported. The search is case-insensitive and supports fuzzy matching.</p>
<p>For example, providing <code>?filter=OS</code> returns enrollments with <code>provider.name</code> containing <code>os</code> or <code>OS</code> (such as <code>Joseph</code>) and Stedi payer IDs containing <code>OS</code>, such as <code>OSBLI</code> for OptumHealth Salt Lake County.</p></div></div><div class="text-sm border-t openapi-property scroll-mt-32 w-full text-blue-700 dark:text-blue-300 break-all whitespace-normal inline-flex items-center gap-1"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" leading-[24px]"><p>Sort the results by one or more properties. By default, Stedi sorts results by the <code>createdAt</code> property in descending order.</p>
<p>Supply a query string with each property appended using <code>&amp;</code>. Each property must be provided in a <code>property:direction</code> format, where <code>property</code> is the name of the property to sort by and <code>direction</code> is the sort direction, either <code>asc</code> (ascending) or <code>desc</code> (descending).</p>
<ul>
<li>When you don&#x27;t include <code>id</code>, Stedi automatically adds it as the final sort criterion to ensure deterministic results.</li>
<li>When you provide multiple properties, Stedi sorts by their order in the query string. For example, if you provide <code>?sortBy=updatedAt:desc&amp;sortBy=id:asc</code>, Stedi sorts first by <code>updatedAt</code> in descending order. If multiple records share the same <code>updatedAt</code> date, Stedi then sorts those records by <code>id</code> in ascending order.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Supported properties:</strong> <code>updatedAt</code>, <code>statusLastUpdatedAt</code>, <code>id</code>, <code>requestedEffectiveDate</code></p>
<p>Examples:</p>
<ul>
<li>Sort by <code>updatedAt</code> in descending order: <code>?sortBy=updatedAt:desc</code></li>
<li>Sort by <code>statusLastUpdatedAt</code> in ascending order: <code>?sortBy=statusLastUpdatedAt:asc</code></li>
<li>Sort by <code>updatedAt</code> and then by <code>id</code>: <code>?sortBy=updatedAt:desc&amp;sortBy=id:asc</code></li>
</ul></div></div></div><nav class="api-section-nav"><div class="flex gap-4 items-center"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" text-red-700 dark:text-red-300 whitespace-nowrap break-all" data-component-part="field-required-pill">Required</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>The status of the enrollment.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>DRAFT</code> - You are still editing the record and it has not been submitted to Stedi.</li>
<li><code>STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED</code> - You have submitted the enrollment and it is ready for Stedi to begin processing.</li>
<li><code>PROVIDER_ACTION_REQUIRED</code> - The enrollment requires action from the healthcare provider to proceed, such as providing additional documentation. Stedi will add a note to your enrollment request with clear instructions.</li>
<li><code>SUBMITTED</code> - (Deprecated) Legacy status being phased out in favor of the more specific action-required statuses.</li>
<li><code>PROVISIONING</code> - Stedi has begun the process of completing the enrollment with the payer.</li>
<li><code>LIVE</code> - The enrollment process is complete, and the specified provider can begin exchanging the listed transaction types with the payer.</li>
<li><code>REJECTED</code> - The payer rejected the enrollment. Common reasons for rejection include incorrect details in the request and that the provider is not credentialed with the payer. Customer support will contact you with reasons for rejection and next steps.</li>
<li><code>CANCELED</code> - The enrollment has been terminated per customer or provider request.</li>
</ul><div><section class="rounded-md border bg-fd-card"><div class="flex flex-wrap justify-between p-3 border-t border-b first:border-t-0 last:rounded-b-md first:rounded-t-md"><div aria-level="1" first:border-t-0"><div><code>SUBMITTED</code></div></div><div class="flex flex-col gap-1 p-3 border-t first:border-t-0"><div><code>PROVISIONING</code></div></div><div class="flex flex-col gap-1 p-3 border-t first:border-t-0"><div><code>LIVE</code></div></div><div class="flex flex-col gap-1 p-3 border-t first:border-t-0"><div><code>REJECTED</code></div></div></div><div class="p-3 border-t"><button class="text-sm text-fd-primary/60 hover:text-fd-primary/80 cursor-pointer font-medium">View <!-- -->3<!-- --> more item<!-- -->s</button></div></section></div></div></div><div class="text-sm border-t openapi-property scroll-mt-32 w-full p-3 border-x bg-fd-card first:rounded-t-none last:border-b overflow-visible [role=tabpanel]_&amp;:!border-none [role=tabpanel]_&amp;:!p-0 status of the enrollment.\n  - `DRAFT` - You are still editing the record and it has not been submitted to Stedi.\n  - `STEDI_ACTION_REQUIRED` - You have submitted the enrollment and it is ready for Stedi to begin processing.\n  - `PROVIDER_ACTION_REQUIRED` - The enrollment requires action from the healthcare provider to proceed, such as providing additional documentation. Stedi will add a note to your enrollment request with clear instructions.\n  - `SUBMITTED` - (Deprecated) Legacy status being phased out in favor of the more specific action-required statuses.\n  - `PROVISIONING` - Stedi has begun the process of completing the enrollment with the payer.\n  - `LIVE` - The enrollment process is complete, and the specified provider can begin exchanging the listed transaction types with the payer.\n  - `REJECTED` - The payer rejected the enrollment. Common reasons for rejection include incorrect details in the request and that the provider is not credentialed with the payer.
